  <script type="text/javascript">
    (function() {
        var contextPath = '/jira';
        var eventBuffer = [];

        function printDeprecatedMsg() {
            if (console && console.warn) {
                console.warn('DEPRECATED JS - contextPath global variable has been deprecated since 7.4.0. Use `wrm/context-path` module instead.');
            }
        }

        function sendEvent(analytics, postfix) {
            analytics.send({
                name: 'js.globals.contextPath.' + postfix
            });
        }

        function sendDeprecatedEvent(postfix) {
            try {
                var analytics = require('jira/analytics');
                if (eventBuffer.length) {
                    eventBuffer.forEach(function(value) {
                        sendEvent(analytics, value);
                    });
                    eventBuffer = [];
                }

                if (postfix) {
                    sendEvent(analytics, postfix);
                }
            } catch(ex) {
                eventBuffer.push(postfix);
                setTimeout(sendDeprecatedEvent, 1000);
            }
        }

        Object.defineProperty(window, 'contextPath', {
            get: function() {
                printDeprecatedMsg();
                sendDeprecatedEvent('get');
                return contextPath;
            },
            set: function(value) {
                printDeprecatedMsg();
                sendDeprecatedEvent('set');
                contextPath = value;
            }
        });
    })();

</script>

               <div id="descriptionmodule_heading" class="mod-header">
                <ul class="ops"></ul>
                <h2 class="toggle-title">Description</h2>
               </div>
               <div class="mod-content">
                <div id="description-val" class="field-ignore-highlight"> 
                 <div class="user-content-block"> 
                  <p>Trying to use CollapsingQParserPlugin with facet tagging throws an exception. </p> 
                  <div class="code panel" style="border-width: 1px;">
                   <div class="codeContent panelContent"> 
                    <pre class="code-java"> ModifiableSolrParams params = <span class="code-keyword">new</span> ModifiableSolrParams();
    params.add(<span class="code-quote">"q"</span>, <span class="code-quote">"*:*"</span>);
    params.add(<span class="code-quote">"fq"</span>, <span class="code-quote">"{!collapse field=group_s}"</span>);
    params.add(<span class="code-quote">"defType"</span>, <span class="code-quote">"edismax"</span>);
    params.add(<span class="code-quote">"bf"</span>, <span class="code-quote">"field(test_ti)"</span>);
    params.add(<span class="code-quote">"fq"</span>,<span class="code-quote">"{!tag=test_ti}test_ti:5"</span>);
    params.add(<span class="code-quote">"facet"</span>,<span class="code-quote">"<span class="code-keyword">true</span>"</span>);
    params.add(<span class="code-quote">"facet.field"</span>,<span class="code-quote">"{!ex=test_ti}test_ti"</span>);
    assertQ(req(params), <span class="code-quote">"*[count(<span class="code-comment">//doc)=1]"</span>, <span class="code-quote">"//doc[./<span class="code-object">int</span>[@name=<span class="code-quote">'test_ti'</span>]=<span class="code-quote">'5'</span>]"</span>);</span>
</pre> 
                   </div>
                  </div> 
                 </div> 
                </div> 
               </div>
              </div>

\u003cspan class=\'commentdate_13819224_concise subText\'\u003e\u003cspan class=\'date user-tz\' title=\'11\\/Nov\\/13 19:02\'\u003e\u003ctime class=\'livestamp\' datetime=\'2013-11-11T19:02:07+0000\'\u003e11\\/Nov\\/13 19:02\u003c\\/time\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e                    David, \\n\\n Here is the flow as I see it with the patch: \\n1) The intitial search executes and produces a result based on collapsing the groups by score. \\n2) The facet component needs to regenerate the docset because of the tag\\/exclude parameters. But the scorer is not present when regenerating the docset, so it is using logic that overwrites the group-head each time. used to generate the search results. \\n\\n To keep these in sync you would need to have step 2, also collapse based on score.              \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n
